    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

      AppleID.auth.init({

        scope : 'name email',

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3415175992?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Julie Barrett" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Julie Barrett" href="/user/show/3023796-julie-barrett">Julie Barrett</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/41807637-it-s-a-storm-without-god-it-s-the-perfect-journey-when-you-know-the-n">review of another edition</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3415175992" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10055219255983801561">It's A Storm Without God by Larry Taylor<br/>Book starts with a dedication page then table of contents. Foreword is given by his aunt who cared for him for many years of his life.<br/>Acknowledgements are included. Poem and introduction are included.<br/>Story about how Larry has encompassed God in his life. He recalls back to when he was just a very young baby and some events that took place.<br/>With the demise of the family unit the kids are removed and some stay together, others go to live with other relatives.</span>
  <span id="freeText10055219255983801561" style="display:none">It's A Storm Without God by Larry Taylor<br />Book starts with a dedication page then table of contents. Foreword is given by his aunt who cared for him for many years of his life.<br />Acknowledgements are included. Poem and introduction are included.<br />Story about how Larry has encompassed God in his life. He recalls back to when he was just a very young baby and some events that took place.<br />With the demise of the family unit the kids are removed and some stay together, others go to live with other relatives.<br />Things seem fine but only for a short time before the kids are relocated to another foster home. Cycle goes on and on.<br />As the author speaks of other family members he lets you know he could write a book on them only, maybe in the future?<br />Interesting the passages he uses that bring him to his life today and how accomplished he is.<br />Yearly chronicle of events occur and are discussed. Special remarks are listed at the end of the story: quotes, Bible passages, songs and his morning and night prayers.<br />Received this review copy from the publicist and this is my honest opinion.<br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="10055219255983801561" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText10506191931276312993" style="display:none">A survivor’s journal<br /><br />Ohio born author Larry Eugene Taylor Jr. earned his education from Kentucky State University, has been a successful college level football player, single parent, and is an entrepreneur, a motivational speaker touring the country to stimulate business development and economic empowerment.<br /><br />In a brief but stimulating book Larry shares his life experiences – a difficult childhood from a broken home and living in foster homes, a struggle with addiction, a cancer survivor – and how in every struggle he acknowledges that God protected him and provided a new path for him to overcome obstacles and succeed as the entrepreneur and motivational speaker he has become. Larry offers his thoughts on many aspects of his life journey, and in doing so provides a supportive resource for understanding his frequent appraisal that God’s so Great! He adds pertinent scripture references and even songs that supported him along the way.<br /><br />Larry’s excitement and enthusiasm are contagious and his book lifts the spirit. This is yet another success for the author whose mission is to be a disciple of God’s power and influence. The book is short in length but long in supportive testimony. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_3508937502" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3508937502" />
    <a title="Maurice Agim" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/87980546-maurice-agim"><img alt="Maurice Agim" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1539439005p2/87980546.jpg" /></a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maurice Agim" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maurice Agim" href="/user/show/87980546-maurice-agim">Maurice Agim</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer3508937502&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3508937502" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer484456836773269577">It's A Storm without God is the personal story of Larry Taylor's struggles through life and how he overcame it in the end with the help of God.<br/><br/>Starting from his adolescence up through his teenage days, he narrates how he was taken away from his mother,to his first and second foster homes where they were mistreated. His younger sibling took most of the ass whopping due to his unique juvenile behaviour. With the help of child services, they were finally relocated to another foster home where God w</span>
  <span id="freeText484456836773269577" style="display:none">It's A Storm without God is the personal story of Larry Taylor's struggles through life and how he overcame it in the end with the help of God.<br /><br />Starting from his adolescence up through his teenage days, he narrates how he was taken away from his mother,to his first and second foster homes where they were mistreated. His younger sibling took most of the ass whopping due to his unique juvenile behaviour. With the help of child services, they were finally relocated to another foster home where God was truly present there. GOD'S SO GREAT!!!<br /><br />Being back and forth with his mum and dad at various times growing up, he grew to be addicted to alcohol and drugs. Realising this was not the way to live life, he started to withdraw from them. The withdrawal had the effect of him being paranoid, hysterical, recurrent seizures and major hallucinations resulting to his being hospitalized.<br />Told by doctors he has but 48 hours to live, he found God in the midst of it all who helped him out of his hallucinations and bewilderment. God even inspired him to make inventions, making business plans resulting in his being an entrepreneur. He praises God through out the book and ends it with select songs and Bible verses that help inspire him through out his new journey alongside prayers and beautiful quotes.<br /><br />As an African reader I couldn't understand why he didn't explain the reason his mum and dad got separated from them at such a young age or why he and his siblings got taken away from their mum untill "she got clean and healthy". I however appreciate the helpfulness of the extended family especially Aunt Barbara in helping him and his siblings through it all and their God mother, Amy. One only needs to wonder what would have become of them if the aforementioned developed an I don't care attitude. GOD'S SO GREAT!!!</span>
  <a data-text-id="484456836773269577" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>


      <div class="reviewFooter uitext buttons">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('W7aBGI8v8ee+dBv37R3Qbwf5+peUURsOI1IV5zqsp5ZZ57/PMclu+AEBkHIlpCI8O39ZlpYABBqS+M46F0kwZQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zMjBSPvgNw8GzQMmQmqZusc8fo6UAj46gZ+FCxASKr/Omf+fRQaoELm4iKOK02vp+7rdj5ZTIS4wNV7WPfe9TA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>

She sees them—literally, and had been seeing the dead ever since she can remember. She tried telling her parents about it when she was a child, but they’d vehemently dismissed it to imaginary friends, so she’d stopped talking about it. There were only two people who actually knew Nonie’s secret and knew she was the real deal. One was Buggy Mouton, her best friend since kindergarten, and the other was Guy Skinard, whom Nonie considered her one true love since the day she’d laid eyes on him in high school. Buggy now worked at MeeMaw’s Café off of Main in Clay Point, and Guy, as usual, remained ever at her side—the only difference being he’d died in a freak boating accident nine years ago. Still the prankster even in death, Guy loved causing chaos, especially with men Nonie occasionally dated. She could only imagine what mayhem he might stir up while mirroring her at the funeral home and mingling with the newly departed.Only hours into the first day of her new job, pandemonium engulfs the funeral home, and much to Nonie’s surprise, it has nothing to do with Guy. It’s brought on by the family they’re serving. Seventy-two–year-old Dover Fontenot, the Major of Clay Point, dies in a car accident after indulging in a little extra-curricular activity—only the activity wasn’t with his wife , Hazel. And when Dover’s mistress, Anna Mae Turner, shows up at the funeral home for the visitation hell’s gates rip open and Broussard’s Funeral Home suddenly turns into a geriatric war zone.Amidst the flying hairpieces, canes and curses, Nonie’s best friend, Buggy, decides to drop by the funeral home with news she can’t wait to share. A cable network in New Orleans wants to put together a paranormal investigation team and have them check out purported haunted locations in Louisiana. For every location with solid filming potential, each member of the team gets a five hundred dollar pay check. And Buggy knows without question that if anyone can sniff out the ‘restless’ dead, it’s Nonie.Knowing nothing about paranormal investigation, but lured by the sound of the adventure and the dollar signs circling through her head, Nonie agrees to become part of the Boo Krewe, the name Buggy has formally given the makeshift team.The lure of money may be one thing, but what Nonie doesn’t realize is that occasionally the dead, so excited that someone can actually see and hear them, decide to follow her home, into her bed—the bathroom—the shower. And adding to this new-found frustration, Nonie barely finishes her first investigation when she gets a visit from Anna Mae Turner—the mayor’s former mistress—now dead, as well, and harassingly       var newTip = new Tip($('bookCover_22881898'), "\n\n  <h2><a class=\"readable bookTitle\" href=\"https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/22881898-shot-down?from_choice=false&amp;from_home_module=false\">Shot Down: The True Story of Pilot Howard Snyder and the Crew of the B-17 Susan Ruth<\/a><\/h2>\n\n      <div>\n        by <a class=\"authorName\" href=\"/author/show/9876016.Steve_Snyder?a=9&amp;origin=related_works\">Steve Snyder<\/a><span title=\"Goodreads Author!\">*<\/span>\n      <\/div>\n\n          <div class=\"smallText uitext darkGreyText\">\n            <span class=\"minirating\"><span class=\"stars staticStars notranslate\"><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p10\"><\/span><span size=\"12x12\" class=\"staticStar p3\"><\/span><\/span> 4.31 avg rating &mdash; 13,470 ratings<\/span>            &mdash; published 2014\n          <\/div>\n\n    <div class=\"addBookTipDescription\">\n      \n<span id=\"freeTextContainer10056146887570664413\">\n  Belgium ... February 8, 1944 ... Shot Down and Alive\nFor the first time, the full and complete story of the B-17 Flying Fortress Susan Ruth is shared in unbelievable detail. Author Steve Snyder’s story of his father, Lieutenant Howard Snyder, and <\/span>\n  <span id=\"freeText10056146887570664413\" style=\"display:none\">\n  Belgium ... February 8, 1944 ... Shot Down and Alive\nFor the first time, the full and complete story of the B-17 Flying Fortress Susan Ruth is shared in unbelievable detail. Author Steve Snyder’s story of his father, Lieutenant Howard Snyder, and the Susan Ruth crew, provides in-depth details about many aspects of World War II few understand or know about including the:• separation for young families as men went off to war;• training before heading to foreign soil;• military combat operations;• underground and resistance and what Lt. Snyder did when he joined it;• German atrocities toward captured crew and civilians;• behind-the-scenes stories of the Belgium civilians who risked all to save American flyers who were in the air one moment, spiraling down in flames the next;• creation and dedication of the monument to the Susan Ruth and its crew located in Macquenoise, Belgium in 1989.Shot Down was created from the vast number of letters and journals of Howard Snyder; diaries of men and women on the ground who rescued, sheltered and hid the crew; and interviews conducted by historians. Centered around the 306th Bomb Group in Thurleigh, England, it is informative, insightful and captivating.For most, 70 years is a long time ago. World War II fades in importance as each year goes by.
